03723 
03724 
03725 
03726 WCHAR ff_convert (  /* Converted code, 0 means conversion error */
03727     WCHAR   src,    /* Character code to be converted */
03728     UINT    dir     /* 0: Unicode to OEMCP, 1: OEMCP to Unicode */
03729 )
03730 {
03731     const WCHAR *p;
03732     WCHAR c;
03733     int i, n, li, hi;
03734 
03735 
03736     if (src <= 0x80) {  /* ASCII */
03737         c = src;
03738     } else {
03739 #if !_TINY_TABLE
03740         if (dir) {      /* OEMCP to unicode */
03741             p = sjis2uni;
03742             hi = sizeof(sjis2uni) / 4 - 1;
03743         } else {        /* Unicode to OEMCP */
03744             p = uni2sjis;
03745             hi = sizeof(uni2sjis) / 4 - 1;
03746         }
03747         li = 0;
03748         for (n = 16; n; n--) {
03749             i = li + (hi - li) / 2;
03750             if (src == p[i * 2]) break;
03751             if (src > p[i * 2])
03752                 li = i;
03753             else
03754                 hi = i;
03755         }
03756         c = n ? p[i * 2 + 1] : 0;
03757 #else
03758         if (dir) {      /* OEMCP to unicode (Incremental search)*/
03759             p = &uni2sjis[1];
03760             do {
03761                 c = *p;
03762                 p += 2;
03763             } while (c && c != src);
03764             p -= 3;
03765             c = *p;
03766         } else {        /* Unicode to OEMCP */
03767             li = 0; hi = sizeof(uni2sjis) / 4 - 1;
03768             for (n = 16; n; n--) {
03769                 i = li + (hi - li) / 2;
03770                 if (src == uni2sjis[i * 2]) break;
03771                 if (src > uni2sjis[i * 2])
03772                     li = i;
03773                 else
03774                     hi = i;
03775             }
03776             c = n ? uni2sjis[i * 2 + 1] : 0;
03777         }
03778 #endif
03779     }
03780 
03781     return c;
03782 }
03783
